- [✓] **E5.4: E5 — Phone/Calls (VoIP): pure-Rust SIP softphone (dialer + call log) + incoming-call HUD/toast; reuse mde-voice-hud / mde-voice-config** *(DONE 2026-06-07 — VOIP-28 engine §3-complete across 4 slices; live 2-device round-trip = bench)*
  **DONE (2026-06-07) — the pure-Rust SIP softphone is §3-complete (4 slices, 52 crate tests):** slice 1 REGISTER+digest (`fd678946`), slice 2 outbound INVITE/SDP/ACK/BYE + Call button (`1cf67775`), slice 3 RTP/G.711 + cpal duplex media (`d74d92df`), slice 4 inbound persistent agent + Answer/Decline HUD + `notify-send` toast + `recents` call-log (`fbd9323f`). Acceptance #1 (register + place outbound) + #2 (inbound HUD + toast + call-log) + #3 (graceful no-SIP/no-audio degrade — honest `NoAccount`/`Failed`, never panics) are **code-§3-complete**; the literal "PJSIP" in #1 is **superseded** by the operator's pure-Rust decision ([[e5-4-voip-pure-rust-sip]]). #4's "era-gated on `Theme::Windows10`" is **obsolete under Carbon-only** (no Win10 era; the HUD themes via its own `theme.rs`). The live registrar + 2-device call round-trip (audible RTP, real inbound) is the **post-release SIP-server/HW bench** per [[bench-gates-lifted]].
  **ARCHITECTURE DECISION (operator, 2026-06-07): build VOIP-28 on a PURE-RUST SIP stack, NOT PJSIP** — see [[e5-4-voip-pure-rust-sip]]. The acceptance text says "registers via PJSIP", but PJSIP is a C library and conflicts with CLAUDE.md §1's pure-Rust lock (rustls/cosmic-text, no C deps); this decision **supersedes the "PJSIP" wording**. Surfaced during the 2026-06-07 full-drain `/goal`.
  **BUILD PLAN (pure-Rust SIP engine — multi-slice, §3 no-stub):** `mde-voice-hud` today has NO SIP/RTP deps (iced+serde only); the HUD/keypad/`recents`/`resolve`/`roster` + `mde-voice-config` (kamailio/rtpengine gen) are built; the unbuilt part is the signaling+media engine. Slices: **(1)** SIP signaling crate — `rsip` (parse/build) over a UDP transport + digest auth → real **REGISTER**, replacing the hardcoded `REGISTRATION_STATUS = "Not registered"` with live registration state in the HUD topbar (first §3-reachable slice; live registrar = bench). **(2)** outbound **INVITE/ACK/BYE** + SDP offer/answer driven from the dialer. **(3)** RTP media path (a pure-Rust RTP crate + G.711 PCMU/PCMA for the floor, Opus via the existing audio chain) + ALSA capture/playback. **(4)** inbound INVITE → incoming-call HUD (answer/decline) + Action-Center toast + call-log entry. Each slice lands runtime-reachable (`mde-voice-hud`); the live call round-trip stays the SIP-server bench per [[bench-gates-lifted]]. New deps (`rsip` + RTP/SDP) require a crates.io fetch (network).
  **PROGRESS (2026-06-07) — slices 1–3 DONE; the complete OUTBOUND softphone is real:**
    - **[✓] Slice 1 (`fd678946`):** `sip.rs` — `SipAccount` (loaded from `~/.config/mde/voice/account.toml`) + a real **REGISTER over UDP** with RFC 2617/7616 digest auth (`rsip` parse + `DigestGenerator`); the hardcoded `REGISTRATION_STATUS` placeholder is replaced by live `RegistrationState` driven off the boot Task (tokio `spawn_blocking`). 9 unit tests.
    - **[✓] Slice 2 (`1cf67775`):** outbound **INVITE/SDP/ACK/BYE** — `place_call` (digest retry, 1xx/486/603 handling, SDP-answer parse → remote RTP endpoint) + `hang_up` (BYE); a **Call/Hang-up button** wired to the dialer shows live `CallState`. 6 unit tests.
    - **[✓] Slice 3 (`d74d92df`):** `media.rs` — **G.711 µ-law/A-law + RTP (RFC 3550)** (pure, 5 tests) + a **cpal duplex media engine** (`start_media`/`MediaSession`) that binds the negotiated RTP port, runs mic→G.711→RTP send + RTP→G.711→speaker recv in 20 ms frames; started on call-connect, stopped on hang-up. `cpal` reused from the workspace (mde-musicd). 48 crate tests green.
    - **[ ] Slice 4 — inbound:** the remaining piece. Needs a **persistent SIP agent** (a background thread owning a stable SIP socket that registers + re-registers + listens, so the registrar can forward inbound INVITEs to the Contact) bridged to the HUD via an iced subscription, plus the answer/decline UI, Action-Center toast (`mde toast`), and `recents` call-log write. A larger architectural addition than the outbound slices (which used per-action ephemeral sockets). The RTP socket (`media.rs`) + SIP sockets (`sip.rs`) are allow-listed in `lint-public-ports` (outbound, `connect()`-ed, overlay-routed — not listeners).
  **Audit (2026-06-07):** the dialer HUD is built (`mde-voice-hud`: number display + 3×4 keypad + resolved-chip strip), BUT `REGISTRATION_STATUS = "Not registered"` is a hardcoded honest placeholder — **the PJSIP register/call/inbound wiring is genuinely unbuilt (VOIP-28)**. Lifting the bench gate means *build* VOIP-28 (the native PJSIP register/call/inbound integration) — substantial SIP-client work — THEN the live-call round-trip is the SIP-server bench (post-release). Not a reclassify; real remaining code.
  **AUDIT (2026-06-05) — substantially prebuilt; PJSIP behaviors are the bench.** `mde-voice-hud` (VOIP-27) is a built layer-shell dialer HUD — keypad + dialer-input filtering (`is_dialer_char`/`filter_dialer_chars`), `recents.rs` call-log with empty-state, `resolve.rs` roster-resolved chips, `roster.rs`, and `mde-voice-config` (762 lines, kamailio/rtpengine config gen) — **28 tests, no stubs**. The acceptance bullets (#1 register-via-PJSIP + place-call, #2 inbound HUD + toast, #3 graceful no-SIP) are **all live-SIP-observable → the bench** (a running kamailio/rtpengine + a SIP peer); `mde phone --calls` isn't wired but the standalone `mde-voice-hud` app satisfies the "or the Phone/Calls app" entry. **Mockup fix (commit `bc46d092`):** the topbar hardcoded a fake "Registered · 127.0.0.1:5060" status (+ "Operator"/"BT"/green-available pip) — a §3 violation claiming a registration that didn't exist; replaced with the real host identity (`/etc/hostname`), derived initials, an offline pip, and an honest "Not registered" (VOIP-28 wires the live registrar over the Bus = bench). *Remaining: the VOIP-28+ PJSIP register/call/inbound engine wiring + the `mde phone --calls` shell entry — all SIP-server bench.*
  **As** a user, **I want** a softphone with a dialer, call log, and an incoming-call HUD, **so that** I place and answer VoIP calls from the desktop.
  *Reuse:* `mde-voice-hud` (adapt: PJSIP softphone → Win10 Phone/Calls + HUD); `mde-voice-config` (as-is: kamailio/rtpengine config gen). *Deps:* E4.8 (Action Center toasts).
  **Acceptance** (runtime-observable):
    - [ ] `mde phone --calls` (or the Phone/Calls app) shows a working dialer that registers via PJSIP and places an outbound call; the call log lists prior calls resolved against the roster.

- [✓] **PANEL-POLISH: E5.5 follow-ups — panel.rs enhancements the dead applets had (not regressions)** *(DONE 2026-06-05: mesh-status chip re-homed into panel.rs; OSDs already covered by swayosd-client in labwc rc.xml)*
  After the E5.5 applet-ecosystem retirement, add to the canonical `panel.rs` (these lived only in the dead `mde-panel` host, so they're new shell features, not regressions):
    - [✓] **mesh-status tray chip — DONE (2026-06-05).** New `crates/shell/mde/src/mesh_status.rs`: a background thread (`start() -> Handle`) polls `action/nebula/status` over the Bus every 10 s (800 ms timeout, own current-thread runtime — like `connect.rs`), parsing `StatusSnapshot` → `MeshStatus { peer_count, online }` (online = `active_transport != "offline"`) into shared `Arc<Mutex>` state. `panel.rs` copies it each tick (cheap, non-blocking — mirrors the tray read) and renders a `mesh_chip` (lan-connect/disconnect glyph + peer count) in the indicator row, clicking opens the Workbench mesh view; hidden until the first poll. 3 unit tests (parse online/offline/error-envelope); 181 mde tests pass, fmt + clippy clean. *(Live peer-count = Bus bench.)*
    - [✓] **volume-osd / brightness-osd — ALREADY COVERED (2026-06-05), not a gap.** labwc's vendored `rc.xml` already binds the media keys (`XF86AudioRaiseVolume`/`MonBrightnessUp`/…) to **`swayosd-client`** (a proper on-screen volume/brightness bar) with a raw-tool fallback (`wpctl`/`brightness.sh`) when swayosd is absent. So the deleted `volume-osd`/`brightness-osd` applets were redundant with swayosd — the OSD works without them, no re-home needed. **PANEL-POLISH fully resolved → E5.5/E0.17/E5.6 complete.**
  **As** a user, **I want** one integrated panel (no separate applet host), **so that** status/quick-toggles live in the taskbar/tray, not a duplicate Phase-E host. *Reuse:* the integrated `mde` shell (panel.rs/action_center/net_flyout/task_view/wallpaper/notifyd/tray). *Deps:* E4.4 (taskbar/tray) + E4.8 (Action Center) — both done; E0.17 (panel-canonical decision) — done.
  **Acceptance** (runtime-observable):
    - [ ] Each applet backend (audio/network/brightness/clock/mesh-status/notifications/etc.) renders as a live taskbar tray item with its real value, with no separate applet-host process running.
    - [ ] Toggle-style applets surface as Action-Center quick-action tiles whose state reflects and drives the underlying backend (click toggles, tile state updates).
    - [ ] Mesh/peer-touching applets (mesh-status, network) degrade gracefully with no mesh / no peers (cached state, Bus timeouts, never panic).
    - [ ] Reachable from the `mde panel` / `mde action-center` paths; themed only via `palette::color()`, no raw hex; metrics via `metrics::UI_PX`; era-gated on `Theme::Windows10`.

- [✓] **E5.6: E5 — Retire mde-drawer: confirm quick-actions live in the Action Center, then delete the crate** *(DONE 2026-06-05: `crates/legacy/mde-drawer` git-rm'd in the E0.17/E5.5 coordinated deletion; quick-actions live in `action_center.rs`'s toggle tiles. The `mde-applet-drawer` RPM install + %files were removed too.)*
  **As** a maintainer, **I want** mde-drawer retired once its quick-actions are proven in the Action Center, **so that** there is one quick-action surface and no dead crate.
  *Reuse:* `mde-drawer` (retire-absorb: quick-actions → Win10 Action Center tiles). *Deps:* E5.5, E4.8 (Action Center).
  **Acceptance** (runtime-observable):
    - [ ] Every quick-action previously exposed by mde-drawer is reachable and functional as an Action-Center tile (verified by toggling each and observing backend effect).
    - [ ] No surface invokes or links `mde-drawer`; the crate is removed from `crates/legacy` and the workspace, and `cargo check --workspace` passes with it gone.
    - [ ] No `mde drawer` (or equivalent) subcommand remains dispatchable after retirement.

### E6 — Workbench Re-skin (sequenced last, after M1)
_Depends: E0, E1, E3, E4, E5_

- [✓] **E6.1: E6 — Workbench shell reskin: Manage-Your-Server layout (role cards + action links + Tools/See-also sidebar); Start tile + "Manage Workstation" app with deep-links (mde workbench --page X)** *(DONE 2026-06-07)*
  **DONE (2026-06-07) — Carbon chrome reskin closed slice 2.** The "restyle onto mde-ui" framing was unreachable (the workbench is iced 0.14 vs mde-ui's 0.13 pin — see the E6.10 drift note), so the reskin landed where it actually lives: **`mde_theme::Palette` was moved from Classic-ChromeOS to IBM Carbon** — `dark()` → Gray 100 / `light()` → Gray 10, accent → Carbon Blue 60, support roles → Green 50 / Red 60 / Yellow 30, all matching the shell's `mde-ui` Carbon single-source (carbondesignsystem.com; §2.2 pinning tests rewritten to the Carbon values in the same commit). Since every workbench panel (and `mde-files`/`mde-music`/`mde-peer-card`/`mde-iced-components`) themes through `Palette`, this converts the **whole workbench to Carbon at the one edge** — no era gate needed (Carbon-only, E9.7). No raw hex (design-tokens gate clean; the stale ChromeOS hex-in-comment allowlist entries for palette.rs/app.rs were removed). The era-gating clause in the old acceptance is retired by the Carbon-only decision ([[epic-carbon-design-system-scope]]). All consumer suites green (mde-theme 157, workbench 777, mde-files 194, +others). **Advances E9.7 too** (workbench area → Carbon).
  **ARCHITECTURE MAPPED + PLAN (2026-06-05).** The workbench is its own `mde-workbench` binary (1670-line Iced `App` in `app.rs`), **not** an `mde <sub>` multiplex path; it takes `--focus <group>[.<panel>]` (the existing deep-link, `model::view_from_focus_slug`), NOT `--page` yet. **What already exists (reuse, don't rebuild):** `model::Group` (the 9 roles Dashboard/Apps/Devices/Fleet/LookAndFeel/Maintain/Network/System/Help with slugs+labels+`sidebar_groups()` = all−Network per E4.15), `model::nav_model()` (group→`Vec<Panel>` — these panels become each role card's **action-links**), and `view_from_focus_slug` routing. **The gap to fill:** (a) the workbench has **no `mde-ui` dep** (uses its own `patternfly.rs` chrome + `mde_theme::Palette`); (b) most group-root landing views render a **`"part of the next workbench rollout"` placeholder** (`app.rs::panel_body` catch-all ~L1242 — itself a §3 "coming soon" anti-pattern) instead of a real role card; (c) no role **descriptions** / **Tools·See-also** data; (d) no `--page` alias, Start tile, or "Manage Workstation" .desktop. **Available widgets:** `mde_iced_components::object_card`, `mde-ui` `palette::color`/`metrics::UI_PX`(=11)/`font`/`widget`. **Preview harness confirmed runnable headlessly here** (nested sway; sway/grim/slurp present, live `WAYLAND_DISPLAY`) → the visual half is §3-verifiable in this env. **Slice plan (each its own §3-complete commit, squash at E6 close):**
    1. **[✓] Role metadata + role-card landing (DONE 2026-06-05).** New `crates/workbench/mde-workbench/src/role.rs`: per-`Group` one-line task-oriented description + a `See also` related-role list + `role_landing(group)` rendering the **role card** — icon+title header, description, a **Tasks** action-link list built from `nav_model` panels (each → the existing `Message::SelectPanel`), and a **See also** sidebar (each → the existing `Message::SelectGroup`). Wired in `app.rs::panel_body`: the catch-all now routes every `View::Group(g)` (Apps/Devices/Fleet/Look&Feel/System, + Network when deep-linked) to `role_landing`, **replacing the old "group landing isn't ready yet" placeholder** (a §3 coming-soon surface); Dashboard/Maintain/Help keep their bespoke landings, per-panel not-yet-shipped views keep the friendly empty-state. No new dep needed — the workbench already pulls `mde-theme`(iced)+`mde-iced-components`; themed purely through `Palette` tokens (no raw hex), reusing the shipped hub-tile button/svg idiom. **4 role tests green** (every group has a description; see-also non-empty + excludes self; role icons distinct; `role_landing` constructs for all 9) + full workbench suite builds; fmt/clippy clean. *Pixel capture deferred to the slice-2/3 chrome-reskin visual pass: ad-hoc headless `mde-workbench` capture isn't viable in this sandbox (detached compositors get SIGTERM'd); the card uses only already-proven primitives, so construction tests + clean build are the slice bar.*
    2. **`--page <role>` CLI alias [✓] (DONE 2026-06-05); chrome reskin — REMAINING.** Added `mde-workbench --page <role>` as the role-level deep-link alias of `--focus` (`Cli::target()` prefers the more-specific `--focus`, falls back to `--page`; both resolve through `model::view_from_focus_slug`, so `--page apps` lands on the Apps role card). 4 bin tests (focus-wins-over-page, page-used-when-focus-absent, none-when-neither, page-role-slug-routes-to-card); `--help` shows the flag. **Remaining for slice 2: the visual chrome reskin** — restyle the surrounding sidebar/header/page-heading onto `mde-ui` palette/metrics, era-gated on `Theme::Windows10` (Carbon/Win2000/BeOS keep `patternfly`). *This is the pixel-heavy part; needs the visual pass (gallery capture is sandbox-limited here — bench/preview-session check).*

Ported the `command_for(kind, verb, name)` argv builder + `verb_applies(verb, state)` from `mde-virtual::app` (Start/Stop subset — VM Stop is a graceful `virsh … shutdown`, container Stop is `podman stop`). Actions run the real command on the iced executor then **re-enumerate** so the list reflects the new state (read back from the hypervisor, never assumed); a missing binary / failed command just leaves state unchanged next enumeration (never panics). +5 tests (verb_applies, row_action, command_for VM/container argv, action/bulk reducer construction).
  **SLICE 3 DONE (2026-06-07) — per-instance CPU/mem sparklines.** New `panels/sparkline.rs` (ported from `mde-virtual::sparkline` onto iced 0.14 — 60-point ring buffer → auto-scaled canvas polyline, pure `push_sample`/`spark_points` tested). ComputePanel now keeps a per-instance `InstanceMetrics` ring buffer (CPU% + mem%), sampled every 2 s by a `sample_subscription()` that App::subscription adds **only while Compute is in view** (no polling elsewhere). Sampling is two commands/tick covering all instances: `podman stats --no-stream --format json` (direct CPU%/MemPerc) + `virsh -c qemu:///system domstats --cpu-total --balloon` (cumulative `cpu.time` → % by delta over the 2 s window via the pure `cpu_percent_from_delta`; mem% = balloon.current/maximum). Pure parsers `parse_podman_stats`/`parse_domstats_cpu_mem`/`parse_percent` all tested; missing tools / stopped instances → flat sparkline, never an error. Each row renders the CPU (success-green) + mem (accent) spark pair. +7 tests.

Steps: name (with live sanitize + validation + start-from-template picker reading `…/mde/vm-templates/*.json` with apply/delete) → resources (vCPU/RAM steppers, clamped) → disk + installer-ISO (scan `/var/lib/mde-vms/isos`, custom-path field, MeshFS toggle) → review. `CreateRequest::virt_install_command()` maps the resolved spec to a real `virt-install --connect qemu:///system …` argv (`--cdrom` with an ISO, else `--import`). Wired into ComputePanel: a "+ New VM" header button opens it, the wizard owns the body while open, and Create issues the real virt-install then re-enumerates. +9 wizard tests (validation/sanitize/step-gating/stepper-clamp/template-apply-clamp/effective-iso/argv-mapping) + 1 panel test (open→cancel).

  **As** a new node operator, **I want** the first-run to also pick my deployment role, enrol me on the Nebula mesh, optionally pair my phone, and make me read the disclaimer, **so that** one OOBE pass both sets up the desktop and joins the node to the fleet.
  *Reuse:* `mde-wizard` Birthright pages + `mde-installer` `Profile` (adapt — fold into OOBE), platform CA/enrollment + `mackes-nebula-https-tunnel` (as-is), `mde-kdc`/`mde-kdc-proto` (adapt/as-is), `disclaimer.rs` `include_str!` (new glue). *Deps:* E7.1, E2.2, E6.1.

- [✓] **E7.3: E7 — `mde birthright` commissioning dashboard shell + lifecycle + Desktop section** *(DONE 2026-06-08)*
  Design: `docs/design/birthright-commissioning.md` (operator 20-Q survey, 2026-06-08). New `crates/shell/mde/src/birthright.rs` + `"birthright"` dispatch arm; full-window iced app (about.rs harness), Carbon via `palette::color()` + `metrics`, role-gated Workstation-only through `role_gate::DESKTOP_ONLY`. Live Desktop section (tri-state + checking) re-probing every 2s via an `iced::time::every` subscription + a manual "Re-check all"; OOBE `Msg::Finish` hands off via `launch_birthright` (Workstation, non-dry, best-effort — never strands `oobe_done`); skel `autostart` re-launches `mde birthright --autostart`, which self-gates on the per-user `state.birthright_show_at_startup` flag (default ON, unchecked via the footer checkbox → atomic `save()`). Captured to `tests/accuracy/captures/gallery/birthright.png` (compositor OK / panel X / services ! — the black-desktop regression is exactly what the panel row catches). 10 new tests; 177 mde + 31 mde-session green; clippy/fmt clean.
  **Decision (§6):** the per-user `birthright_show_at_startup` flag in `~/.config/mde` is the single operative re-surface gate; a separate root-owned `/var/lib/mde` machine-first-boot marker was dropped — a per-user desktop session can't cleanly write `/var/lib/mde`, and the per-user flag fully satisfies "surfaces on first boot, keeps reopening until unchecked". Applet-registration sub-check was dropped in favour of the clipboard-daemon lockfile probe (panel renders applets in-process, so there is no separate applet process to observe; the daemon lock is the honest "autostart ran" proxy). The Mesh/Voice/Network cards are NOT rendered as placeholders (CLAUDE.md §3 — no mockups); they land live in E7.4/E7.5. The fix-button + mde-bus event path are the Mesh section's concern (E7.4); E7.3's Desktop checks are cheap `/proc` scans driven by the time subscription + Re-check.
  **As** an operator who just installed a Workstation, **I want** a commissioning screen that opens at the end of OOBE and again at each login until I uncheck it, confirming the full desktop is actually built, **so that** I have positive proof the box came up whole rather than the black-desktop failure mode.
  *Reuse:* `oobe.rs` Finalize hand-off, the skel `autostart` first-run block (like `mde setup`), `~/.config/mde` state (`#[serde(default)]`, atomic `save()`), `clipboard::dir()` daemon-lock probe + labwc/panel `/proc` scan. *Deps:* E7.2, E8 (held release reads it).

- [✓] **E7.4: E7 — birthright Mesh section (per-component rows + remediation)** *(DONE 2026-06-08 — verified against the live mackesd on the dev box)*
  Per-component live mesh rows over `mde-bus`, reading `mackesd` health, with fix buttons. Built on E7.3's shell. A background poller thread (`start_mesh_poller`, mirroring `mesh_status::start`) re-probes every 5s with 800ms-timeout Bus RPCs off the UI thread; the 2s UI tick reads the shared `Arc<Mutex<Option<MeshProbe>>>` snapshot; manual Re-check + post-fix fire a one-shot `refresh_mesh`. Four rows: **mde-bus** (`Persist::open` reachability), **mackesd** (`action/shell/healthz` → HealthReport — version/node_count/audit_chain/unreachable), **Nebula** (`action/nebula/status` → online/offline), **LizardFS** (`action/meshfs/status` → master_reachable/offline_peers). Fix buttons run real commands (`fix_argv`, unit-tested): Start mackesd = `systemctl --user start mackesd` (mackesd is a user unit), Re-enroll = re-exec `mde oobe` (E7.2's enrolment stage), Open Workbench = `mde-workbench`.
  **Decision (§6):** "mackesd (+ each worker)" is rendered as one mackesd row off `healthz` (the live-probe `action/shell/workers` roster is available but the per-worker breakdown adds rows without changing the commissioning verdict — folded into the mackesd detail line). LizardFS "Mount" remediation became "Open Workbench" (the mesh storage control surface) — a direct user-session mount needs a bootstrapped master + privilege (bench), whereas Workbench is the real reachable surface that drives it. mde-bus liveness is a local `Persist::open` (the Bus is a file-backed store); if it can't open, every row fails with that reason (`MeshProbe::all_fail`).
  **As** a node operator, **I want** the dashboard to show each mesh component's health separately with a way to fix a red one, **so that** I can confirm (and recover) mackesd, the Nebula overlay, the LizardFS mount, and the Bus in one place.
  *Reuse:* `mackesd` `health.rs` `HealthReport` (via `action/shell/healthz`), `mesh_status` Bus-RPC pattern, `mde_bus::rpc::request`, E7.2 OOBE enrolment flow (Re-enroll). *Deps:* E7.3, E3 (LizardFS), E7.2.
  **Acceptance** (runtime-observable):
    - [✓] The Mesh card shows independent Pass/Degraded/Fail/checking rows for `mackesd`, the Nebula overlay, LizardFS, and `mde-bus`; values come from `mackesd` over `mde-bus` and refresh on the 5s poller + manual Re-check. *(gallery verified: live mackesd → "v10.0.0 up", bus OK)*
    - [✓] Each failed/degraded row offers a contextual fix: Start mackesd (`systemctl --user start mackesd`), Open Workbench (LizardFS), **Re-enroll** (re-execs `mde oobe`, E7.2's enrolment); `fix_argv` is unit-tested and the press spawns the real command + nudges a re-probe. *(see Decision re Mount→Workbench)*
    - [✓] Degraded is distinct from Fail (overlay offline / master-unreachable render Degraded; a missing RPC reply renders Fail); no raw hex (palette `STATUS_*` roles), metrics via `metrics`. *(gallery verified: Nebula + LizardFS amber, not red)*
    - [✓] Reachable from `mde birthright`; degrades gracefully on Bus timeout / mackesd down (`MeshProbe::all_fail` + per-row Fail reasons, never panic — the poller thread isolates the 800ms RPC stalls). *(8 new parse/argv tests; 12 birthright tests total)*

- [✓] **E7.5: E7 — birthright Voice section + the SIP-over-Bus plumbing it needs** *(DONE 2026-06-08; split from the Network half → E7.5b)*
  The Voice attestation row + the cross-process SIP status it required. Originally bundled with Network; **re-split** because the Voice half had a real blocker (the E5.4 SIP agent's state lived only inside the `mde-voice-hud` process) — operator chose (2026-06-08) to **build the SIP-over-Bus plumbing** rather than ship a proxy or defer.
  Built: (1) `mde-voice-hud` `sip.rs` now publishes a timestamped `state/voice/status` snapshot (`{registered,listening,server,detail,ts}`) to the Bus on each registration change + a 15s heartbeat (`publish_voice_status`, sync `Persist::write` — no runtime on the agent thread); (2) a headless **`mde-voice-hud --agent`** mode (`run_headless_agent`) that runs the persistent register+listen loop with no GUI and publishes status (honest "Not registered" heartbeat when no `account.toml`), launched from the skel `autostart`; (3) birthright's **Voice** card reads the retained `state/voice/status` (sync `Persist::list_since`), treating a heartbeat older than `VOICE_STALE_SECS` (45s) as "agent not running" — registered+listening → Pass, listening-only → Degraded, else/stale/absent → Fail, with a "Voice settings" fix (`mde-voice-config`). The birthright poller was generalised mesh→`LiveProbe{mesh,voice}` (one Bus-reading thread serves both).
  **Decision (§6):** the live registered-against-a-real-registrar Pass is the **SIP-server bench** (per [[e5-4-voip-pure-rust-sip]] + [[bench-gates-lifted]]); everything else is §3-complete and **verified live on the dev box** — the headless agent published `state/voice/status` and birthright read+rendered it ("Softphone (SIP): not listening (Not registered)"). The inbound-call→answer/decline HUD hand-off stays E5.4's domain (the headless agent logs the ring; it does not own the GUI handoff). A loopback test-call button is deferred to the bench too.
  **As** an operator, **I want** the dashboard to prove the softphone is up (registered + listening), **so that** I can confirm voice at commissioning.
  *Reuse:* E5.4 persistent SIP agent (`sip::run_agent`), `mde_bus` (`Persist::write`/`list_since`), `mde-voice-config` (fix). *Deps:* E7.3, E5.4.
  **Acceptance** (runtime-observable):
    - [✓] The Voice card shows Pass only when the agent reports **registered AND listening**; listening-without-registration is Degraded; absent/stale status is Fail; a non-green row offers a "Voice settings" fix. *(parse_voice unit-tested for all states; live gallery shows the honest no-account Fail)*
    - [✓] The agent's registration + listener state is published to the Bus (`state/voice/status`, heartbeated + timestamped) by a headless `mde-voice-hud --agent` autostarted at login, so birthright reads it cross-process. *(verified: agent created the `state/` topic + birthright rendered its value)*
    - [✓] The Voice row renders live tri-state, refreshing on the poller + manual Re-check; reachable from `mde birthright`, palette `STATUS_*` roles, degrades gracefully (stale/no-bus → Fail, never panic). *(4 new birthright tests + 1 sip test; 15 birthright + 54 voice-hud + 187 mde green; clippy/fmt clean)*

- [✓] **E7.5b: E7 — birthright Network section (network-tool readout)** *(DONE 2026-06-08 — verified live)*
  Three live network rows on the `LiveProbe` poller: **Internet (NetworkManager)** via `crate::nm::active_connections` (nmcli, non-loopback active conns), **Mesh peers (roster)** via `action/nebula/list-peers` (`Vec<PeerRow>` → paired/online counts), and **LAN scan (netassess)** read from the latest stored `~/.local/share/mde/netassess/<host>/<iso>-<hash>.json` (ARP host count + scan stamp). Network rows added to `LiveProbe.network`; the NM + LAN-scan rows also populate on a Bus-down `all_fail` (they're local, not Bus-backed).
  **Decision (§6):** dropped the **Fleet** row — `action/fleet/*` is a Phase-G stub (always the not-implemented envelope), so surfacing it would be a §3 mockup. Standalone per-peer **RTT** has no Bus endpoint (the `StatusSnapshot`/`PeerRow` expose reachable state, not latency), so the roster row reports paired/online counts instead of RTT. The **LAN scan is read-only** of the netassess worker's latest report (the worker owns the scan cadence) rather than triggering nmap from the dashboard — avoids a privileged/long nmap on the UI path; the auto-poll only reads the cheap stored report.
  **As** an operator, **I want** the dashboard to surface the platform's network readouts, **so that** I can confirm connectivity + reachability at commissioning.
  *Reuse:* `crate::nm::active_connections`, `action/nebula/list-peers`, the netassess report files. *Deps:* E7.5.
  **Acceptance** (runtime-observable):
    - [✓] The Network card surfaces network-tool readouts — NetworkManager active connections, the Nebula peer roster (paired/online), and the latest LAN (netassess) scan; the expensive nmap is the worker's job (read-only here), so the poll stays cheap. *(gallery verified live: "1 active: Wired connection 2", "no paired peers yet", "0 LAN host(s) seen")*
    - [✓] Rows render live tri-state via the `LiveProbe` poller + manual Re-check; reachable from `mde birthright`, palette roles only, degrades gracefully when a tool/daemon is absent (Bus-down still shows NM + LAN locally; never panic). *(2 new tests; 17 birthright + 187 mde green; clippy/fmt clean)*

- [✓] **E7.6: E7 — birthright report export (Copy diagnostics + Save report)** *(DONE 2026-06-08; escalation split → E7.6b)*
  The commissioning-record half of the attestation extras. `build_report` serializes all four sections' rows (`{check,status,detail}`) into pretty JSON with a `{product,host,generated_ts}` header; "Copy diagnostics" pipes it to `wl-copy`, "Save report" writes `~/.local/share/mde/birthright/<ts>-commissioning.json`. - [✓] **E7.6b: E7 — birthright post-commissioning escalation (panel badge + toast)** *(DONE 2026-06-08 — closes the E7 birthright epic)*
  The panel gains a post-dismissal health watch. `start_health_watch` (a background thread mirroring `mesh_status::start`) polls `birthright::health_summary` every 30s **only when `birthright_show_at_startup == false`** (so the dashboard owns first-boot; the watch is the after-dismissal safety net) and writes a per-section roll-up to a shared `HealthHandle`. Each panel tick reads it through the pure `health_transitions(summary, &mut alerted)`: a section's green→red edge toasts once via `notify-send` (notifyd serves FDO `org.freedesktop.Notifications`), recovery re-arms it, and a stuck-red subsystem never re-toasts. A flat "!" `health_badge` (risk-coloured ASCII, no nerd-glyph tofu) shows in the tray while anything is non-green and re-opens `mde birthright` on click.
  **Decision (§6):** the badge is plain ASCII "!" (not a nerd glyph) to guarantee no tofu (§2.4 covers SVG icons, not raw panel font chars). The watch reuses `birthright::health_summary` (the same probes the dashboard uses), so the panel + dashboard agree on what's green. The live green→red trigger is observable on the running desktop (uncheck show-at-startup, stop a service → badge + toast); the debounce/no-spam contract is unit-tested headlessly (`health_transitions_toast_once_per_edge_no_spam`).
  **As** an operator who dismissed the dashboard, **I want** to be told if something I'd confirmed later breaks, **so that** I don't silently lose a subsystem.
  *Reuse:* `panel.rs` tray + tick, `birthright::health_summary` (shared probes), `notify-send` → `notifyd` (FDO). *Deps:* E7.6.
  **Acceptance** (runtime-observable):
    - [✓] After the startup flag is unchecked, a regression of a previously-green subsystem raises a panel health badge (steady while non-green) + a single debounced toast per green→red edge deep-linking to `mde birthright`; a flapping peer does not toast-spam. *(health_transitions unit-tested: toast-once, recover-rearm, no-spam, Degraded counts; badge wired to Launch("mde birthright"))*
    - [✓] Reachable from the panel; palette `STATUS_RISK` role only; degrades gracefully (no Bus / probe failure → rows Fail, watch never panics; badge is tofu-free ASCII). *(8 panel + 192 mde tests green; clippy/fmt/lint-gates clean; panel gallery no-regression)*

- [✓] **E8.2: E8 — Disclaimer audit sweep across every About/Info/Help surface (single-source verified)** *(DONE to floor 2026-06-05 — every surface single-sources `mde_disclaimer`; no copy-paste; GUI render-match = display bench)*

  **AUDIT (2026-06-05).** Swept the tree: **all disclaimer text resolves through `mde_disclaimer`** (the `mde-disclaimer` crate's build-time `include_str!` of the repo-root `DISCLAIMER.md`), and **no copy-pasted disclaimer literal exists** in any `.rs` (grepped a distinctive `DISCLAIMER.md` phrase across `crates/` outside the source crate → zero hits). The two surfaces that render the full disclaimer today both single-source: (1) shell **`mde about`** → `about.rs` → `crate::disclaimer::view()`, and `crates/shell/mde/src/disclaimer.rs` is a thin `pub use mde_disclaimer::TEXT` + `view()` re-export; (2) the **Workbench About** panel (E6.9) → `mde_disclaimer::TEXT`, locked by `about.rs::about_renders_the_single_source_disclaimer`. Only `workbench` + `shell/mde` dep `mde-disclaimer` — correct, since they own the only two disclaimer surfaces that exist. **Remaining (re-audit at release):** the OOBE "read before proceeding" step (**E7.2**, not built) and any installer/daemon-banner surface must also single-source when they land; this task closes once E5/E6/E7's surfaces are complete (per its `Deps: E4,E5,E6,E7`). Existing-surface acceptance #1/#2 ✓ now; #3 (live edit→rebuild propagation) is inherent to `include_str!` single-sourcing.

  *Reuse:* `disclaimer.rs` `include_str!` (single source) at `crates/shell/mde/src/disclaimer.rs`. *Deps:* E4, E5, E6, E7.

    - [✓] A sweep proves every such surface resolves its text through `disclaimer.rs` `include_str!`; no surface embeds a copy-pasted literal of the disclaimer. *(swept 2026-06-05 — zero copy-paste; all via `mde_disclaimer`)*

- [✓] **E8.3: E8 — Promote clippy todo + unwrap_used to deny; full cargo clippy --all-targets / fmt --check / test green workspace-wide** *(DONE 2026-06-08 — `1c49050c`)*

### HW — Hardware / Interactive Bench (post-release, release-gated — NOT task blockers)
_Depends: feature code complete_

- [ ] **HW-1: KDE Connect real-phone round-trip (notifications/messages/photos/calls bidirectional)**
  **As** the operator, **I want** a real paired phone to exchange notifications, SMS, photos and call events both ways over the finished inbound listener (3b.2e), **so that** the Win10 "Your Phone" surface is proven against actual hardware, not loopback.
  *Reuse:* crates/kdc/mde-kdc-host + mde-kdc-proto (as-is/adapt, §9). *Deps:* E2.1.
  **Acceptance** (runtime-observable):
    - [ ] A phone notification appears as an E3 toast filtered to the KDE Connect device, and dismissing it on the desktop clears it on the phone.
    - [ ] An SMS sent from the Your Phone "Messages" pane is received on the phone, and an inbound SMS appears in the pane without a manual refresh.
    - [ ] A photo pushed from the phone lands in the Photos pane and opens; a desktop file shared to the phone arrives in its share sheet.
    - [ ] An incoming phone call raises the call HUD and a "decline/mute" action from the desktop takes effect on the phone; mutual-TLS fingerprint pin holds (no fallback to unpinned).

- [ ] **HW-2: BlueZ pairing on real hardware**
  **As** the operator, **I want** to power, discover, pair, connect and remove a real Bluetooth peripheral from the Settings Bluetooth pane, **so that** the BlueZ-via-zbus wiring is confirmed on bench radios.
  *Reuse:* mde-applets Settings Bluetooth pane (adapt, §9) over BlueZ zbus. *Deps:* none.
  **Acceptance** (runtime-observable):
    - [ ] Toggling the radio in the pane powers the adapter on/off and the system tray Bluetooth glyph reflects the new state.
    - [ ] A live scan lists a nearby device; selecting it completes pairing (PIN/confirm prompt where required) and it shows Connected.
    - [ ] An input or audio device routes through after connect (keystrokes register / audio plays), and Remove unpairs it so it disappears from the paired list.

- [ ] **HW-3: PAM unlock + argon2 PIN on real hardware**
  **As** the operator, **I want** `mde lock` (Win+L) to unlock with both an argon2 PIN and a PAM password on real keyboards, **so that** the lock face is proven against the live auth stack, not a stub.
  *Reuse:* mde lock layer-shell lock face + argon2 (`~/.config/mde/pin.hash`), PAM (§10). *Deps:* none.
  **Acceptance** (runtime-observable):
    - [ ] Win+L raises the layer-shell lock face and the session is genuinely locked (input to apps behind it is blocked).
    - [ ] A correct argon2 PIN unlocks and returns to the exact prior session; a wrong PIN is rejected and re-prompts.
    - [ ] Switching to password and entering the real account password unlocks via PAM; an incorrect password is rejected by PAM with no panic.

- [ ] **HW-4: dnf live-streaming Windows Update on real hardware**
  **As** the operator, **I want** the Win10 "Windows Update" surface to drive a real dnf transaction with live-streamed progress, **so that** package output is confirmed flowing to the UI on actual repos/network.
  *Reuse:* Settings/Update surface over dnf (§10). *Deps:* none.
  **Acceptance** (runtime-observable):
    - [ ] "Check for updates" runs a real dnf metadata refresh and the surface lists actual available package counts.
    - [ ] Starting an update streams per-package download/install lines into the UI in real time (not a single end-of-run dump).
    - [ ] A completed transaction shows success state and the installed version is reflected on a follow-up check; a network drop mid-stream surfaces an honest error, never a hang.

- [ ] **HW-5: Compositor/session cutover + greeter: all 3 roles boot -> greeter -> usable session on bench hardware** [!]
  **As** the operator, **I want** each deployment role to boot through its greeter into a usable session on real GPUs, **so that** the labwc/session cutover (a standing real-HW risk) is validated per role.
  *Reuse:* mde-session (launch labwc) + greetd/regreet/cage; LightDM-gtk win10() theme (as-is/adapt, §10/§12). *Deps:* E1.5.
  **Acceptance** (runtime-observable):
    - [ ] Workstation boots to the themed greeter, login starts labwc, and the Win10 taskbar/Start are interactive on the bench display.
    - [ ] Server (headless) reaches a usable login/console with its worker subset up and no display-manager spawned.
    - [ ] Lighthouse boots with enrollment-CA/Bus/Nebula only — no greeter, no desktop — and accepts an enrollment.
    - [ ] Logout/restart/shutdown from the session returns cleanly to greeter or powers down without a stuck compositor.

- [ ] **HW-6: LizardFS mesh-storage across a multi-peer fleet (replication + offline degrade)**
  **As** the operator, **I want** mesh XDG dirs replicated across a multi-peer LizardFS fleet and to confirm graceful degrade when peers drop, **so that** topology-aware replication and offline behavior are proven on real nodes.
  *Reuse:* mackesd meshfs worker (LizardFS FUSE) + LizardFS master/chunk (§11/§12). *Deps:* E3.1.
  **Acceptance** (runtime-observable):
    - [ ] A file written on one peer's mesh dir appears on a second peer's mount within the replication goal.
    - [ ] Killing a chunk peer leaves the file readable from a surviving replica; rejoining the peer re-replicates and the goal count is restored.
    - [ ] With all peers offline the mount serves cached state and surfaces degrade gracefully with no mesh / no peers (cached state, Bus timeouts, never panic).

- [ ] **HW-7: VoIP real outbound/inbound call via Vitelity**
  **As** the operator, **I want** to place and receive a real PSTN call through the Vitelity trunk from the Phone/Calls app, **so that** the kamailio/rtpengine softphone path is proven end-to-end with two-way audio.
  *Reuse:* mde-voice-hud Phone/Calls app + mde-voice-config (kamailio/rtpengine) (adapt/as-is, §9). *Deps:* none.
  **Acceptance** (runtime-observable):
    - [ ] Dialing a real number from the Phone/Calls app connects through the Vitelity trunk with audible two-way audio.
    - [ ] An inbound call to the DID raises the call HUD toast; answering connects two-way audio and hangup tears down the session cleanly.
    - [ ] The completed call lands in the call-history list with correct direction and duration; a registration loss surfaces an honest "not registered" state, never a silent dead dialer.

- [ ] **HW-8: Deployment-role install from media for each role (Lighthouse/Server/Workstation)**
  **As** the operator, **I want** to install from real media and pick each deployment role at the role chooser, **so that** the one-RPM role-chooser provisions the correct worker subset and surfaces per role on bare hardware.
  *Reuse:* mde-installer + deployment-role chooser (adapt, §9/§12). *Deps:* none.
  **Acceptance** (runtime-observable):
    - [ ] Booting the media presents the role chooser and selecting Workstation provisions a system that first-boots into the greeter with the full surface set enabled.
    - [ ] Selecting Server provisions a headless system whose mackesd brings up the fleet/meshfs/metrics worker subset with no display manager.
    - [ ] Selecting Lighthouse provisions a relay node with enrollment-CA/leader/health workers only and a LizardFS read-only client — no media/voice/compute, no greeter.
    - [ ] Each installed role's systemd units and `/etc/mackesd/` templates match the chosen role on first boot (correct worker set running, no role-foreign units active).

### RETIRE-PY — Python-daemon retirement (EPIC-RETIRE-PY-DAEMONS)
_Depends: surfaced by the E0.11 audit (2026-06-03). These are v1.x→v2.0.0 transition shims whose own source comments say "the v2.0.0 cut reimplements [this]" but never landed in the merge. Governance §11 C13. Several converge with other epics — noted per task._

- [✓] **RETIRE-PY.1: RETIRE-PY — Port the mDNS relay worker to native Rust → RESOLVED AS RETIRE (dead/broken worker)**
  **Done (2026-06-05) — retired, not ported (rescue-pass cleanup).** Investigation showed the worker was **broken dead code**, not a live feature to port: it spawned `python3 -m mackes.mesh_mdns`, but **that module does not exist** (only `mackes/mdns_relay.py` does — a different name), so the command fails immediately and `RestartPolicy::OnFailure` would spin it in a restart loop. Even the real `mdns_relay.py` is dead — its `mackes.mesh_sync` substrate was wholesale-retired (DEAD-2.10), so its `put`/`list_keys` are no-ops; its own module comment says the relay is "obviated by mDNS service discovery on the Nebula overlay directly." Nothing in the live Rust tree consumes the relay output, and the promised v2.0.0 `mdns-sd` reimplementation never landed (`mdns.rs` only *named* mdns-sd in a doc comment — it never used it). **Retired:** deleted `workers/mdns.rs` (`MdnsWorker`), its `pub mod`, the `run_serve` spawn block + import, and the `("mdns", 0)` tier entry; also dropped the now-orphaned optional `mdns-sd` dep + its feature gate from `mackesd/Cargo.toml`. Census drops 30→**29** (Lighthouse 11→10, all tiers −1 since mdns was rank 0). **Verified:** 7 worker_role tests pass; `mackesd role-workers` shows 10/13/29 with **no `mdns`**; mackesd builds + fmt clean, no orphaned-dep warning. *The cross-segment mDNS **service** relay (republish peer A's Jellyfin/Chromecast onto peer B's LAN) is a genuine feature that is **not implemented in v10** — filed as a deferred decision below; it needs a new transport (Bus/overlay, the old mesh_sync is gone) + a 2-segment bench, so it is operator-product-direction, not a python-retirement.*

- [✓] **MESH-MDNS-RELAY: E-feature — native cross-LAN-segment mDNS service relay (mackesd worker)** *(operator chose REBUILD 2026-06-05; implemented 2026-06-05 — cross-segment round-trip = post-release peer bench)*
  **As** a user with services on multiple LAN segments, **I want** a peer's mDNS services (Jellyfin/Chromecast/AirPlay/…) to appear on other segments' LANs over the mesh, **so that** discovery works fleet-wide, not just per-segment. *Context:* the v1.x python relay (`mdns_relay.py`) did this via `avahi-browse` + `avahi-publish-service` bridged over `mesh_sync` — both retired (RETIRE-PY.1). **Operator decision (2026-06-05): rebuild natively.** Native plan:
    - **Browse:** a mackesd worker browses the local LAN for the curated relayed service types (`mdns-sd` `ServiceDaemon::browse`, or the existing `discover-mdns`/`avahi-browse` path) — re-add the `mdns-sd` dep RETIRE-PY.1 dropped (it's the real consumer now).
    - **Transport:** publish discovered local services to a Bus topic over the Nebula overlay (e.g. `mesh/mdns/<peer>/<service-type>`, replacing `mesh_sync`); subscribe to other peers' topics.
    - **Republish:** register each *other* peer's services on the LOCAL LAN via `mdns-sd` `ServiceDaemon::register`, **substituting the originating peer's mesh IP for the source LAN IP**, peer-suffixed names to avoid collisions.
    - **Anti-loop:** tag announces with origin-peer-id; never re-broadcast our own.
    - **Type policy (from v1.x §9 lock):** relay `_jellyfin/_googlecast/_airplay/_spotify-connect/_home-assistant/_syncthing/_netdata/_subsonic._tcp`; NEVER `_ipp/_pdl-datastream/_smb/_afpovertcp/_ssh._tcp` (privacy).
  **OUTBOUND HALF DONE (2026-06-05):** new `crates/mesh/mackesd/src/workers/mdns_relay.rs` (`MdnsRelayWorker`, rank 0, registered in `run_serve`). Browses the relayed service types via `mdns_sd::ServiceDaemon` (re-added the `mdns-sd` dep RETIRE-PY.1 dropped — now the real consumer), and on each discovered local service publishes an `MdnsAnnounce { peer=own mesh IP, service, service_type, port, txt }` to the `mesh/mdns/announce` Bus topic (`Persist::write`). **Anti-loop:** skips any service carrying the `mde-relay-origin` TXT (i.e. one WE republished). **Type policy** enforced by `is_relayed` (media allowlist; never ssh/smb/printers). **Graceful degrade:** no `nebula1` IP (pre-enrolment) or no multicast iface → idles until shutdown, never panics; shutdown via an `AtomicBool` stop flag set when the supervisor signals. Census 29→**30** (lighthouse 11). **Verified:** 7 unit tests (allowlist allow/reject, `bare_type` fullname/domain reduction, announce JSON round-trip, `announce_from_info` lift / skip-non-relayed / skip-anti-loop against real `ServiceInfo`s); mackesd builds + fmt + clippy clean; `role-workers` lists `mdns_relay`. **INBOUND HALF DONE (2026-06-05):** the worker's single `run_relay_blocking` loop now does both halves each pass. Inbound: `Persist::list_since(ANNOUNCE_TOPIC, cursor)` polls peers' announces; **drops own-origin** (anti-loop); registers each NEW peer service once (dedup by `peer|type|instance`) via `daemon.register(build_republish_info(ann))` — a `ServiceInfo` advertised at the **peer's mesh IP** (LAN clients connect over the overlay), peer-suffixed instance name, carrying the `mde-relay-origin` TXT so the outbound browse skips it. **+4 inbound unit tests** (republish_name peer-suffix, service_key distinctness, build_republish_info advertises the mesh-IP + origin-tag, rejects a non-IP peer) → **11 total**; builds + fmt + clippy clean. **FEATURE COMPLETE** (browse→publish→subscribe→republish, no python). *(Live mDNS browse + the cross-segment round-trip — peer A's Jellyfin on peer B's LAN — = post-release 2-peer bench per [[release-authorization-and-gates]].)*
  **Acceptance** (runtime-observable): a mackesd worker browses + republishes with **no python**; single-node browse + the parse/map/anti-loop/allowlist logic unit-verified now; **the cross-segment round-trip (peer A's Jellyfin appears on peer B's LAN) is a post-release 2-peer bench** (per the 2026-06-05 [[release-authorization-and-gates]] "hold HW / open peer gates" directive). Degrades gracefully with no mesh/peers (idle browse loop, never panics). *Deps:* E0.3 Bus (done). *Reuse:* `mackesd/src/workers/`, the retired `mdns_relay.py` as the spec, `surrounding_hosts`/`discover-mdns` for the browse idiom.

- [✓] **RETIRE-PY.2: RETIRE-PY — Port the Remmina-profile sync worker to native Rust (replaces `python3 -m mackes.remmina_sync`)**
  **Done (2026-06-05):** rewrote `workers/remmina_sync.rs` from a `SubprocessTickWorker` (spawned `python3 -m mackes.remmina_sync`) into a **native Rust tick worker** — zero python. Every 60 s `RemminaSyncWorker` reads the mesh peer registry (`mackes_mesh_types::peers::read_peers` over `peers_dir(default_mesh_home())` — the Nebula-native `PeerRecord` source, *not* the retired tailscale_status), TCP-probes each peer's :22/:3389/:5900, and reconciles Remmina's `Mesh Peers` group: one `.remmina` per (peer, open proto), SSH using the mesh key (pubkey auth), RDP/VNC blank-cred for the keyring. Add/update/delete is idempotent and **never touches files outside the managed group** (locked Q4 rule). The python's enable/disable/systemd-unit/tweaks surface was the UI/CLI path — out of the worker's scope, dropped. *Best-choice:* connect host = peer `hostname` (PeerRecord carries no IP; resolvable on the overlay) — recorded for a future hostname→Nebula-IP refinement. The tick runs `sync_once` on `spawn_blocking` (TCP+fs are blocking); shutdown via `select!`. **Verified:** 11 unit tests (slug, render ssh/rdp, tcp open/closed against a real listener, group-parse, reconcile add/idempotent-skip/delete/foreign-untouched); mackesd builds clean; fmt + clippy clean (fixed all net-new lints — field docs, format_push_string→single format!, const fns, unit-pattern). Worker stays registered in `run_serve` at the Workstation tier. *(Cross-PEER appearance — profile on A visible on B — is a 2-peer bench; the no-python native sync + reconcile + graceful no-mesh degrade is done.)*
  **As** a user, **I want** Remmina RDP/VNC profiles synced across peers by a native Rust worker, **so that** remote-desktop profile sync needs no Python.
  *Reuse:* `mackesd/src/workers/remmina_sync.rs` (now a native tick worker). *Deps:* none.
  **Acceptance** (runtime-observable):
    - [✓] A Remmina profile created on one peer appears on another with **no** `python3`/`mackes.remmina_sync` spawn. *(Native worker — no python; render+reconcile verified. Cross-peer hop is a 2-peer bench.)*

The **dense inline buttons** (Settings' ~60 per-row Pair/Remove/Set-as-default/Add-device actions, filedialog's toolbar buttons, control-panel's launcher tiles) stay compact — they fall under the worklist's explicit "pragmatic for dense chrome" clause; a 40px button in a dense device/list row reads oversized. Button-height conversion is complete; no further per-button grind.
  - **[✓] Shared component styles complete (2026-06-07):** the `mde-ui` component widgets are all flat Carbon now — `sunken_field`/`sunken_picklist` (focus ring, E9.4), checkbox/radio (Carbon states, E9.4), buttons (`button_primary`/`button_ghost` + the three Carbon heights), modals (dialog chrome flat via the E9.7 `draw_edge`), and **the property-sheet tab control converted to flat Carbon** (`TabEdge` — dropped the Win2000 3D white/silver/gray bevels for a face + 1px border + the 2px accent selected-cue; gallery-verified on system-properties / taskbar-properties). List/menu selection uses the Carbon-remapped `HIGHLIGHT` role.
  - **[>] Remaining E9.3 = the per-surface token migration:** convert each surface's raw `.spacing()`/`.padding()`/`.size()` literals to the `metrics` Carbon tokens (E9.2 substrate), enforced by the **E9.6** lint gate. **Policy:** exact 8px-grid values (2/4/8/12/16/24/32 → `SPACING_01..07`) migrate (pixel-identical); off-grid fine-tuned gaps (3/5/6/10/14, and `0` = no-gap) stay raw as documented pragmatic exceptions (E9.2 clause) — they become the E9.6 allowlist. **Batch 1 (2026-06-07):** `dialogs.rs` (fully — incl. snapping 10→12, 14→16, gallery-verified shut-down), `about.rs`, `system_properties.rs`, `taskbar_properties.rs`, `control_panel.rs` exact-grid spacing/padding → tokens. Build + 183 mde tests green. **Batch 2 (2026-06-07):** exact-grid spacing/padding → tokens across `settings.rs` (109 sites — the now-canonical modern config surface), `display.rs`, `task_view.rs`, `action_center.rs`, `security.rs`, `restore.rs`, `oobe.rs`, `menu.rs`, `packages.rs`, `filedialog.rs`, `search.rs`, `installer.rs`, `net_flyout.rs`, `project.rs`, `phone.rs`, `disclaimer.rs`, `clipboard.rs`, `start_common.rs`, `popup.rs`, `lock.rs` (all pixel-identical → no gallery needed; build + 183 tests green). Excluded: `panel.rs` (dense tray chrome — exception) and `files.rs` (E10 rework pending). **DONE (2026-06-07) — the migration was deeper than batches 1–2 implied (the net-new-only gate had grandfathered the other padding idioms):** the `.size()` font pass was already complete (all via `metrics::*` type tokens, 0 raw literals); the **`Padding::from([…])`/`Padding::from(N)` idiom** (`1480aec3`, 56 pure-exact-grid sites) and the **`pad(t,r,b,l)` helper + `Padding{…}` struct idioms** (`97ecff57`, 24 tuples + 1 struct field) were then converted. Every PURE exact-grid space/size literal in the surfaces now resolves from a Carbon `SPACING_*`/`TYPE_*` token; mixed/off-grid tuples (a 3/5/6/10/14/18/20/… component), 0-gaps, and computed exprs stay raw as the documented E9.2 pragmatic exceptions. **E9.3 surface migration complete.**

- [✓] **E9.5: E9 — Carbon motion tokens** (standard durations + easing for hovers/expansions/toasts). *(DONE 2026-06-07)*
  **Done (2026-06-07):** named the IBM Carbon v11 motion **duration scale** (`DURATION_FAST_01..SLOW_02` = 70/110/150/240/400/700 ms) and **easing curves** (`EASING_STANDARD`/`ENTRANCE`/`EXIT` productive cubic-béziers) in `mde-theme::motion`, pinned by `carbon_duration_scale_is_pinned` + `carbon_easing_curves_and_mapping_are_pinned`. Reconciled the named `Motion` presets to the grid: panel/dialog mount → `moderate-02` (240 ms, was the UX-9 180 ms), tooltip fade → `fast-02` (110 ms, was 120); the notification pulse stays 2 s (a continuous loop, off-grid, documented). The abstract `Easing` enum now maps to the exact Carbon curves via `Easing::carbon_bezier()` (entrances→entrance, exits→exit, standard→standard) so consumers can emit the precise `cubic-bezier`. 156 mde-theme tests green; fmt + clippy clean (no net-new warnings); the existing `lint-motion-tokens` gate still passes. *(Per-animation migration to the named tokens is incremental, like the E9.3 surface migration; the canonical tokens + the main presets are Carbon now.)*

### E10 — Ultimate File Manager (operator epic, 2026-06-06)
_Depends: E9.2 (Carbon substrate), E3 (mesh). Scope locks in memory `epic-ultimate-file-manager-scope`. Subsumes/【retires】the E5.1 split-Explorer plan — one manager remains._

**AUDIT (2026-06-07, full-drain) — E10 is ~80% pre-built (the `mde-files` crate already exists at `crates/services/mde-files`, 9.5k lines, a workspace member that builds + launches no-panic).** Like E9.3/E5.4, the actual code is well ahead of the `[ ]` marks. Confirmed-done items closed below; the real remainder is E10.3 (picker mode), the E10.5 tabs half, and E10.6 (the unification — gated on a feature-parity check vs `files.rs`).

- [✓] **E10.1: E10 — Port `mde-files` UI from libcosmic to iced + iced_layershell** *(DONE — audited 2026-06-07)*
  **DONE.** `crates/services/mde-files` is pure **iced 0.14** (`Cargo.toml` has ZERO `cosmic`/`libcosmic` deps — only iced + `mde-theme` + `mde-iced-components`); themed via `mde-theme::Palette`. `mde-files` builds + launches no-panic. *(NOTE: it landed on iced **0.14**, not the acceptance's "0.13" — so it can't fold into the iced-0.13 `mde` binary; the unification is via `mde files` exec'ing the `mde-files` binary, see E10.6. The standalone binary is Carbon-themed via `mde-theme`, the workbench's decoupled palette edge.)*
- [✓] **E10.2: E10 — Replace `demo_data.rs` with the real filesystem/mesh backend** *(DONE — audited 2026-06-07)*
  **DONE.** `app.rs` defaults to `RealBackend::new()` = `LocalFsBackend` (real fs) + `Option<BusBackend>` (D-Bus, 800 ms timeout) + `Option<MeshBackend>` (mesh, 800 ms timeout) — graceful when Bus/mesh absent. `DemoBackend`/`demo_data.rs` are **test-only** (every ref is `#[cfg(test)]` / `with_backend`), i.e. test scaffolding, NOT a shipped mockup — so §3 ("no mockup passing as a feature") holds. *(The literal "delete the mock" is satisfied in spirit: production reads real data; the demo stays as a unit-test fixture.)*
- [✓] **E10.3: E10 — Fold the Open/Save dialog (`filedialog`) onto the one engine** *(DONE 2026-06-08 — `66cc9332`)*
  **DONE.** Added a **`--pick` chooser mode** to `mde-files` (`picker.rs`): a self-contained iced 0.14 Open/Save dialog that lists through the SAME engine the manager browses with (`LocalFsBackend::list_dir`) in the classic dialog grammar (Look-in ancestors, quick-access places, folders-first filtered list, File name + Files-of-type rows), honouring the exact CLI contract (`--save`/`--title`/`--dir`/`--filename`/`--filter`) — prints the chosen path to stdout, exits 0 (non-zero on Cancel). `main.rs` routes `--pick` to it. The shell's **`filedialog.rs` is repointed** to prefer `mde-files --pick` when installed (`exec` passes stdout + exit code straight through), falling back to the in-shell Carbon dialog on headless roles (role_gate requires `filedialog` everywhere) — no capability regression. 4 picker unit tests (filter parse, folders-first listing, target resolution); app boots to the iced event loop under `--pick`. **Surfaced finding (tracked):** `mde-files` themes from the Material-indigo `tokens.css` (and amber PF_* dev-fallback), **not IBM Carbon** (§1) — a pre-existing crate-wide gap. **Fully retiring the in-shell `filedialog.rs`** (deleting the Carbon fallback) is gated on mde-files reaching Carbon parity → see the new E10.7 item.
- [✓] **E10.4: E10 — Mesh-first features first-class** (mesh sidebar, send-to-peer, LizardFS browse — the Artifact Manager thesis). *(DONE to floor — audited 2026-06-07)*
  **DONE to floor.** `mesh_backend.rs` (connects the real mesh over the Bus, 800 ms timeout) + `send_to.rs` (send-to-peer: toolbar action + targets) + the mesh sidebar are built; `RealBackend` composes the mesh backend. The live cross-peer browse/send round-trip is the 2-node bench per [[bench-gates-lifted]].
- [✓] **E10.5: E10 — v1 capabilities: tabs + inline archive (zip/tar) handling.** *(DONE 2026-06-08 — `3cead623`)*
  **DONE.** Inline **archive** was already built (`Mime::Archive` for zip/tar/gz/xz/zst/bz2/7z/rar + `ArchiveConflictFile` op flow). **Tabs** now landed: multi-directory browser tabs via the *active-mirror* pattern — `model::Tab` { view, local_path, mesh_home_path, search } holds per-tab nav state; the active tab is mirrored into the flat `MdeFiles` fields so the 1800-line view()/update() is untouched, re-synced each update (`sync_active_tab`) and swapped on switch (`load_active_tab` + the standard `refresh_snapshot` re-list). `views::tab_strip` renders chips (click=switch, ×=close when >1) + a `+` new-tab button above the toolbar; `subscription()` wires Ctrl+T/Ctrl+W/Ctrl+Tab via `event::listen_with`. New/Close/Switch/Cycle keep ≥1 tab + clamp active. 5 reducer tests; 211 mde-files tests green; boots to the iced event loop.
- [✓] **E10.6: E10 — Retire the shell `files.rs` Explorer; repoint the Start-menu "File Explorer" + the `inode/directory` default handler to the unified manager** (no dead code; one manager remains). *(DONE 2026-06-08 — `69c133fe`; mde-files brought to storage-surface parity + files.rs retired)*
  **DONE (2026-06-08, 5 slices):** operator chose "build local browsing + SMB + Cloud-Files into mde-files, then retire files.rs" ([[e10-keep-smb-cloudfiles]]). Built in mde-files: **local browsing** (`7030576c` — FileRow paths, real Local listing, descend/open/copy/up), **Cloud-Files** (`7e75e3b5` — KDC roster over the Bus), **Network + quick-nav** (`3ec2a68f`), **interactive SMB host-browse** (`d093e24c` — `smbclient -L` → mount over GVfs). Then the **unify cut-over** (`69c133fe`): `mde files [PATH]` execs the `mde-files` binary (iced 0.14 vs the shell's 0.13 — process boundary, not in-binary; open_uri + Start-menu follow automatically), `mde-files` accepts a `[PATH]` arg, `row_style` moved to its sole consumer phone.rs, **`files.rs` (2929 lines) git-rm'd** + `mod files` dropped + line-keyed allowlists cleaned. One manager remains; 172 mde tests green. **Follow-on polish (not blocking):** async SMB browse, sftp-browse INTO a cloud device, descend-on-double-click. **→ This also UNBLOCKS E9.7's `Theme::Windows10` variant-finalize (was files.rs-gated).**
  **CRITICAL FINDING (2026-06-07 audit):** `mde-files` **deliberately does NOT browse the local filesystem** — `View::Local` is `views::local_veil`, an explainer placeholder ("the unsynced filesystem… move a file into ~/mesh to share"); `model.rs` locks "the mesh is the home base, not the local filesystem." It's a **mesh Artifact Manager, NOT a local Explorer**. `files.rs` is the opposite (This PC / local disks / folders / SMB / Cloud-Files). Retiring `files.rs` for `mde-files` would drop **all local file browsing** (descent + file-open + FileRow paths are also absent), not just SMB/Cloud-Files. The earlier "port SMB+Cloud-Files in" decision assumed local browsing existed — it doesn't. **NEEDS OPERATOR RE-DECISION** (see [[e10-keep-smb-cloudfiles]]): (a) build full local browsing + SMB + Cloud-Files into mde-files (huge, contradicts its mesh-first thesis); (b) keep BOTH tools (`mde files`=local Explorer, `mde-files`=mesh manager — drop the retire-files.rs goal); (c) hybrid. **RESOLVED 2026-06-08 — operator chose: BUILD LOCAL BROWSING INTO mde-files** + SMB + Cloud-Files, making it a true unified manager, THEN retire `files.rs`. E10.6 UNBLOCKED → status [>]. **PROGRESS (2026-06-08, 3 slices landed):**
  - **[✓] Slice 1 (`7030576c`):** real local browsing — `FileRow.path` (from `LocalFsBackend::list_dir`), `MdeFiles.local_path`/`local_files` refreshed on `View::Local`, `views::local_browser` (replaces the `local_veil`), context-menu **Open** (descend folder / `xdg-open` file) + **Copy Path** (`wl-copy`), `LocalUp`.
  - **[✓] Slice 2 (`7e75e3b5`):** Cloud-Files — `BusBackend::cloud_devices` (`action/connect/devices` KDC roster, pure-decoded by `cloud_rows_from_json`) → `RealBackend::list("cloud:")` → `View::CloudDevices` + sidebar entry. Live phone + sftp-browse = bench/follow-on.
  - **[✓] Slice 3 (`3ec2a68f`):** Network + quick-nav — `Message::LocalGoto(path)`; the sidebar pins now navigate to their real path (were dead-ends); a **Network** entry browses the GVfs mount dir (`mde mount smb://…`-ed shares browse via the local browser).
  - **[✓] (3b) interactive SMB host-browse** (`d093e24c` — typed-host → `smbclient -L` → share list → `mde mount`) **and (4) unify** (`69c133fe` — `mde files` execs the `mde-files` binary, open_uri `inode/directory` + Start-menu follow, `files.rs` deleted). Both landed; see the DONE header above.
  **AUDIT:** `mde files` still dispatches to `files.rs` (2929 lines); `open_uri.rs` references `mde files`. The unification = make `mde files` **exec the `mde-files` binary** (the iced-0.14-vs-0.13 skew rules out an in-binary fold), repoint open_uri's `inode/directory` + the Start-menu entry, then delete `files.rs`. **GATE — feature-parity (RESOLVED 2026-06-07):** `files.rs` carries SMB/Network + Cloud-Files (KDE-Connect sftp) browsing (E5.1 scope) that `mde-files` lacks. **Operator decided: PORT SMB + Cloud-Files INTO mde-files** before retiring `files.rs` (honors the E5.1 subsumed scope; no storage-surface regression) — see [[e10-keep-smb-cloudfiles]]. So E10.6 = **(prereq)** add an SMB/Network browse surface (gio/smbclient, as files.rs did) + a Cloud-Files surface (KDC roster via `connect::devices` over the Bus + sftp) to mde-files, **then** repoint `mde files` to exec the `mde-files` binary, repoint open_uri `inode/directory` + the Start-menu entry, and delete `files.rs`.
- [✓] **E10.7: E10 — Bring `mde-files` onto IBM Carbon (§1 parity)** *(DONE 2026-06-08 — `a35588b5`)*
  **DONE.** `mde-files/theme.rs` re-based onto the IBM Carbon Gray-100 dark palette: surface ramp → Gray 100/90/80/70, text → Gray 10/30/50, accent amber → Blue 50 (button → Blue 60), the amber/rust/indigo tints → Blue 50 tints, status → Green 40/Red 50/Yellow 30 — matching the shell's mde-ui dark mapping + the canonical `mde_theme::Palette::dark()`. `theme()` now builds the Iced base directly from those Carbon constants and **drops the shared Material `tokens.css` read** (that GTK-era path is vestigial — no GTK layer remains — and tokens.css is non-Carbon + shared); removed the orphaned token helpers + the `mackes-theme` dep. Verified at the §3 token floor: 2 pinning tests assert the Gray ramp + Blue accent + support colours + that `theme().palette()` is Carbon; 213 mde-files tests green; clippy/fmt clean; boots to the iced event loop. **Render-observe visual pass = display bench.** **Note:** the in-shell `filedialog.rs` stays as the **headless-role fallback** (mde-files is desktop-only) — its look concern is resolved, but availability keeps it; it is NOT dead code. The other `tokens.css` readers (mde-voice-hud / mde-logout-dialog / mde-popover toasts) are separate surfaces with their own Carbon follow-on, out of this item's scope.
  **FINDING:** the whole `mde-files` crate themes from `data/css/tokens.css` (`cds_bg_default #202124`, `mackes_accent #4285f4` Material-You indigo) with a warm-dark amber `PF_*` dev fallback — **not the IBM Carbon Gray 10/90/100 + Blue 60 lock** (§1). The worklist's earlier "whole workbench/mde-files to Carbon via `mde-theme::Palette`" framing is partly aspirational: `mde-files` has its OWN `theme.rs` (`theme()` reads tokens.css, not `mde_theme::Palette`), so it never picked up the Carbon move. Since `mde-files` is now the one file manager (E10.6) AND the Open/Save picker host (E10.3), this is the platform's most-used non-Carbon surface. **Scope:** re-point `mde-files/theme.rs` onto the Carbon tokens (Gray ramp + Blue 60 accent, light/dark) — single edge, like `mde-ui::palette` — and update `data/css/tokens.css` `cds_*`/`mackes_accent` to Carbon values; the picker + manager + workbench-shared components inherit it. **Then** the in-shell Carbon `filedialog.rs` fallback can be deleted (E10.3 close-out) and `mde files`/`--pick` are fully Carbon. Not release-gating for the *manager* (it ships and works), but it IS the §1 lock — sequence with the E9.2 token rebase.

- [✓] **E9.9: E9 — Carbon-ify the remaining non-Carbon service-crate surfaces (§1 parity)** *(DONE 2026-06-08 — `a1377906`)*
  **DONE.** All three re-based onto IBM Carbon Gray-100 dark + Blue accent: **mde-popover/toasts.rs** (toast Palette + pill accents source `mde_theme::Palette::dark()`; SURFACE_BG → Gray 100), **mde-voice-hud/theme.rs** (Material-3 sub-palette → Carbon ramp + Blue/Green 60/Red 60 FABs; +1 pinning test), **mde-logout-dialog** (dropped the Material `tokens.css` read; `load_theme()` sources `mde_theme::Palette::dark()` directly — removed the orphaned mackes-theme dep + stale allowlist entries). Each builds + clippy/fmt clean; render-observe = display bench. §1 Carbon-only lock now holds across the platform's iced surfaces (the workbench/`mde-theme` consumers were already Carbon; mde-ui shell is Carbon; mde-files E10.7; these three close the remainder).
  **FINDING:** chasing the `tokens.css` readers from E10.7 surfaced three more surfaces still on a pre-Carbon palette (they predate the E9 Carbon-only collapse and never converted), each a §1 violation:
  - **`mde-voice-hud/theme.rs`** — a hand-rolled **Material-3-dark** sub-palette (`SURF #131316`, etc.); the VOIP softphone HUD (E5.4).
  - **`mde-logout-dialog`** — reads the Material-indigo `tokens.css` (same vestigial GTK path E10.7 dropped from mde-files).
  - **`mde-popover/toasts.rs`** — builds an iced `Palette` from raw amber/green/red `Color::from_rgb` literals (also a §2.1 raw-value smell the float-form dodges the hex gate).
  **Scope:** re-base each onto the Carbon Gray-100 dark tokens + Blue accent (the E10.7 pattern — drop the `tokens.css`/Material values, build from Carbon constants, pin with a token test). Each is small + independent. Visual coherence = display bench. Not release-gating individually, but it closes the §1 Carbon-only lock across the platform.
